! Signature
! Description

| ClearToasts
| void ToastAPI.ClearToasts( int32 location )
| Clears the toast panels by location. -1 means 'all' locations
|-
| CreateToast
| void ToastAPI.CreateToast( cstring id, cstring title, cstring message, int32 location, int32 duration, cstring icon, cstring style )
| Creates a Toast panel.
|-
| CreateToast_Custom
| void ToastAPI.CreateToast_Custom( cstring id, cstring layoutFile, int32 location, int32 duration, unknown params )
| Creates a custom Toast panel with a given layout file.
|-
| CreateToast_Simple
| void ToastAPI.CreateToast_Simple( cstring title, cstring message )
| Creates a simple info Toast panel in the top right with default duration.
|-
| DeleteToast
| void ToastAPI.DeleteToast( cstring id )
| Delete an existing toast by ID
|}

== UiToolkitAPI ==
Helper to show popups, tooltips, context menus and to register/invoke js callbacks.
